16x2 easyC LCD Library 1.0.0
This is a library for the 16x2 easyC LCD Module
u-blox_config_keys.h
Go to the documentation of this file.

15 This library handles configuring and handling the responses
16 from a u-blox GPS module. Works with most modules from u-blox including
17 the Zed-F9P, NEO-M8P-2, NEO-M9N, ZOE-M8Q, SAM-M8Q, and many others.
18
19 https://github.com/sparkfun/SparkFun_Ublox_Arduino_Library

22 Arduino IDE 1.8.13

43#ifndef __u_blox_config_keys_h__
44#define __u_blox_config_keys_h__
45
46//The following consts are used to generate KEY values for the advanced protocol functions of VELGET/SET/DEL
47const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_1 = 0x01; //One bit
48const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_8 = 0x02; //One byte
49const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_16 = 0x03; //Two bytes
50const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_32 = 0x04; //Four bytes
51const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_64 = 0x05; //Eight bytes
52
53//These are the Bitfield layers definitions for the UBX-CFG-VALSET message (not to be confused with Bitfield deviceMask in UBX-CFG-CFG)
54const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_RAM = (1 << 0);
55const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_BBR = (1 << 1);
56const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_FLASH = (1 << 2);
57const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_ALL = VAL_LAYER_RAM | VAL_LAYER_BBR | VAL_LAYER_FLASH; //Not valid with getVal()
58
59//Below are various Groups, IDs, and sizes for various settings
60//These can be used to call getVal/setVal/delVal
61//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
62const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_UBX = 0x01;
63const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_NMEA = 0x02;
64const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_RTCM3 = 0x04;
65
66const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2C = 0x51;
67const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2COUTPROT = 0x72;
68const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART1INPROT = 0x73;
69const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART1OUTPROT = 0x74;
70const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART2INPROT = 0x75;
71const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART2OUTPROT = 0x76;
72const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_USBINPROT = 0x77;
73const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_USBOUTPROT = 0x78;
74
75const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART_SIZE = VAL_SIZE_1; //All fields in UART group are currently 1 bit
76const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2C_SIZE = VAL_SIZE_8; //All fields in I2C group are currently 1 byte
77
78const uint8_t VAL_ID_I2C_ADDRESS = 0x01;
79
80//Below are the key values for a given configuration setting
81
82//CFG-BDS: BeiDou system configuration
83//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
84const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_BDS_USE_PRN_1_TO_5 = 0x10340014; // Use BeiDou geostationary satellites (PRN 1-5)
85
86//CFG-GEOFENCE: Geofencing configuration
87//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
88const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_CONFLVL = 0x20240011; // Required confidence level for state evaluation
89const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_PIO = 0x10240012; // Use PIO combined fence state output
90const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_PINPOL = 0x20240013; // PIO pin polarity
91const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_PIN = 0x20240014; // PIO pin number
92const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE1 = 0x10240020; // Use frst geofence
93const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_LAT = 0x40240021; // Latitude of the first geofence circle center
94const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_LON = 0x40240022; // Longitude of the first geofence circle center
95const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_RAD = 0x40240023; // Radius of the first geofence circle
96const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE2 = 0x10240030; // Use second geofence
97const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_LAT = 0x40240031; // Latitude of the second geofence circle center
98const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_LON = 0x40240032; // Longitude of the second geofence circle center
99const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_RAD = 0x40240033; // Radius of the second geofence circle
100const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE3 = 0x10240040; // Use third geofence
101const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_LAT = 0x40240041; // Latitude of the third geofence circle center
102const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_LON = 0x40240042; // Longitude of the third geofence circle center
103const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_RAD = 0x40240043; // Radius of the third geofence circle
104const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE4 = 0x10240050; // Use fourth geofence
105const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_LAT = 0x40240051; // Latitude of the fourth geofence circle center
106const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_LON = 0x40240052; // Longitude of the fourth geofence circle center
107const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_RAD = 0x40240053; // Radius of the fourth geofence circle
108
109//CFG-HW: Hardware configuration
110//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
111const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_VOLTCTRL = 0x10a3002e; // Active antenna voltage control flag
112const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_SHORTDET = 0x10a3002f; // Short antenna detection flag
113const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_SHORTDET_POL = 0x10a30030; // Short antenna detection polarity
114const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_OPENDET = 0x10a30031; // Open antenna detection flag
115const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_OPENDET_POL = 0x10a30032; // Open antenna detection polarity
116const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_PWRDOWN = 0x10a30033; // Power down antenna flag
117const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_PWRDOWN_POL = 0x10a30034; // Power down antenna logic polarity
118const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_RECOVER = 0x10a30035; // Automatic recovery from short state flag
119const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SWITCH_PIN = 0x20a30036; // ANT1 PIO number
120const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SHORT_PIN = 0x20a30037; // ANT0 PIO number
121const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_OPEN_PIN = 0x20a30038; // ANT2 PIO number
122const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_ENGINE = 0x20a30054; // Antenna supervisor engine selection
123const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SHORT_THR = 0x20a30055; // Antenna supervisor MADC engine short detection threshold
124const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_OPEN_THR = 0x20a30056; // Antenna supervisor MADC engine open detection threshold
125
126//CFG-I2C: Configuration of the I2C interface
127//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
128const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_ADDRESS = 0x20510001; // I2C slave address of the receiver (7 bits)
129const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_EXTENDEDTIMEOUT = 0x10510002; // Flag to disable timeouting the interface after 1.5 s
130const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_ENABLED = 0x10510003; // Flag to indicate if the I2C interface should be enabled
131
132//CFG-I2CINPROT: Input protocol configuration of the I2C interface
133//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
134const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_UBX = 0x10710001; // Flag to indicate if UBX should be an input protocol on I2C
135const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_NMEA = 0x10710002; // Flag to indicate if NMEA should be an input protocol on I2C
136const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_RTCM3X = 0x10710004; // Flag to indicate if RTCM3X should be an input protocol on I2C
137const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_SPARTN = 0x10710005; // Flag to indicate if SPARTN should be an input protocol on I2C
138
139//CFG-I2COUTPROT: Output protocol configuration of the I2C interface
140//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
141const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_UBX = 0x10720001; // Flag to indicate if UBX should be an output protocol on I2C
142const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_NMEA = 0x10720002; // Flag to indicate if NMEA should be an output protocol on I2C
143const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_RTCM3X = 0x10720004; // Flag to indicate if RTCM3X should be an output protocol on I2C
144
145//CFG-INFMSG: Information message configuration
146//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
147const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_I2C = 0x20920001; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the I2C interface
148const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_UART1 = 0x20920002; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the UART1 interface
149const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_UART2 = 0x20920003; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the UART2 interface
150const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_USB = 0x20920004; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the USB interface
151const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_SPI = 0x20920005; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the SPI interface
152const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_I2C = 0x20920006; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the I2C interface
153const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_UART1 = 0x20920007; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the UART1 interface
154const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_UART2 = 0x20920008; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the UART2 interface
155const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_USB = 0x20920009; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the USB interface
156const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_SPI = 0x2092000a; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the SPI interface
157
158//CFG-ITFM: Jamming and interference monitor configuration
159//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
160const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_BBTHRESHOLD = 0x20410001; // Broadband jamming detection threshold
161const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_CWTHRESHOLD = 0x20410002; // CW jamming detection threshold
162const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ENABLE = 0x1041000d; // Enable interference detection
163const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ANTSETTING = 0x20410010; // Antenna setting
164const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ENABLE_AUX = 0x10410013; // Scan auxiliary bands
165
166//CFG-LOGFILTER: Data logger configuration
167//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
168const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_RECORD_ENA = 0x10de0002; // Recording enabled
169const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_ONCE_PER_WAKE_UP_ENA = 0x10de0003; // Once per wake up
170const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_APPLY_ALL_FILTERS = 0x10de0004; // Apply all filter settings
171const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_MIN_INTERVAL = 0x30de0005; // Minimum time interval between loggedpositions
172const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_TIME_THRS = 0x30de0006; // Time threshold
173const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_SPEED_THRS = 0x30de0007; // Speed threshold
174const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_POSITION_THRS = 0x40de0008; // Position threshold
175
176//CFG-MOT: Motion detector configuration
177//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
178const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_MOT_GNSSSPEED_THRS = 0x20250038; // GNSS speed threshold below which platform is considered as stationary (a.k.a. static hold threshold)
179const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_MOT_GNSSDIST_THRS = 0x3025003b; // Distance above which GNSS-based stationary motion is exit (a.k.a. static hold distance threshold)
180
